[2026-01-03T17:26:42Z] Pavan Pamidimarri: 4.	The Battle of Zama was a decisive battle fought outside the city of X. X’s forces were led by its legendary and seasoned general Y who pioneered the use of war elephants in the Mediterranean. Many years earlier Y led a campaign across the Alps – elephants and all – into  and to Rome’s doorstep. Scipio Africanus was the young Roman commander who spent years studying Y’s battle tactics. When Y’s elephants began charging, Scipio had his soldiers blow trumpets and horns at full blast. The sudden, ear-splitting noise panicked the elephants. Scipio’s win at Zama sealed the fate of X, resulting in its complete destruction, and Rome’s status as the unchallenged master of the Mediterranean world. ID X and Y.
